Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;

```

        String x;
        x = "foo";
        x += "bar";
        x += "baz";
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 1
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.isAdditive()) {
            Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();
            if (parent instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression && ((ASTAssignmentExpression) parent).isAdditive()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private Set<String> stringVariables = new HashSet<>();

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTLocalVariableDeclaration.class, ASTExpressionStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTLocalVariableDeclaration node, Object data) {
        stringVariables.add(node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableDeclarator.class).getName());
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpressionStatement node, Object data) {
        Node assignmentOperator = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
        if (assignmentOperator != null && assignmentOperator.isAdditive() && isStringVariableUsed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringVariableUsed(ASTExpressionStatement node) {
        String variableName = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableDeclarator.class).getName();
        return stringVariables.contains(variableName);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private Map<String, Integer> stringAppendsMap = new HashMap<>();
    private static final int MAX_CONCATENATIONS = 2;

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceType.class, ASTMethodDeclaration.class, ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceType node, Object data) {
        if (node.getTypeImage().equals("String")) {
            stringAppendsMap.clear();
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        stringAppendsMap.clear();
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentOperator node, Object data) {
        if (node.isCompound()) {
            Node parent = node.jjtGetParent().jjtGetChild(0);
            String variableName = parent.getImage();

            int count = stringAppendsMap.getOrDefault(variableName, 0);
            stringAppendsMap.put(variableName, ++count);

            if (count > MAX_CONCATENATIONS) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2) {
            if (node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess
                    && node.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    private Map<String, Integer> variableUsage;

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTBlock.class);
        variableUsage = new HashMap<>();
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        variableUsage.clear();
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        int numChildren = node.getNumChildren();
        for (int i = 0; i < numChildren; i++) {
            if (node.getChild(i) instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
                ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = (ASTAssignmentExpression) node.getChild(i);
                String variableName = assignmentExpression.getFirstChildOfType(ASTName.class).getImage();
                if (assignmentExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTAdditiveExpression.class)
                        && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAdditiveExpression.class).hasDescendantOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class)) {
                    variableUsage.put(variableName, variableUsage.getOrDefault(variableName, 0) + 1);
                    if (variableUsage.get(variableName) > 1) {
                        addViolation(data, assignmentExpression);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.isCompound()) {
            if (node.jjtGetChild(0).jjtGetChild(0).hasDescendantOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentOperator node, Object data) {
        if (node.isCompound()) {
            Node parent = node.getParent().getParent();
            if (parent instanceof ASTExpressionStatement) {
                Node grandParent = parent.getParent();
                if (grandParent instanceof ASTInfixExpression &&
                        grandParent.jjtGetNumChildren() == 3 &&
                        grandParent.jjtGetChild(0).jjtGetChild(0).toString().equals("StringLiteral")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTLocalVariableDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTLocalVariableDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (node.getType() == String.class) {
            JavaNode n = (JavaNode) node.jjtGetParent();
            for (int i = 0; i < n.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
                Node child = n.jjtGetChild(i);
                if (child instanceof ASTExpressionStatement) {
                    ASTExpressionStatement es = (ASTExpressionStatement) child;
                    if (es.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTAssignmentOperator) {
                        ASTAssignmentOperator ao = (ASTAssignmentOperator) es.jjtGetChild(0);
                        if (ao.isCompound()) {
                            if (ao.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                                ASTInfixExpression ie = (ASTInfixExpression) ao.jjtGetChild(0);
                                if (ie.isStringAdd()) {
                                    addViolation(data, node);
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.isCompound()) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (infixExpression != null && "+".equals(infixExpression.getOperator())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private Map<String, Integer> stringAppendsMap = new HashMap<>();

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        stringAppendsMap.clear();
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentOperator node, Object data) {
        if (node.isCompound()) {
            Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();
            if (parent != null && parent.jjtGetNumChildren() > 0) {
                Node grandchild = parent.jjtGetChild(0);
                if (grandchild instanceof ASTName) {
                    String variableName = ((ASTName) grandchild).getImage();
                    Integer count = stringAppendsMap.get(variableName);
                    if (count == null) {
                        count = 1;
                    } else {
                        count++;
                    }
                    stringAppendsMap.put(variableName, count);
                    if (count > 1) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private Map<String, Integer> stringAppendsCount;

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
        stringAppendsCount = new HashMap<>();
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        Node child = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTBlock.class);
        return visitChild(child, data);
    }

    private Object visitChild(Node node, Object data) {
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            Node child = node.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (child instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
                ASTAssignmentExpression assignment = (ASTAssignmentExpression) child;
                if (assignment.isAdditive()) {
                    String variableName = assignment.jjtGetChild(0).getImage();
                    stringAppendsCount.put(variableName, stringAppendsCount.getOrDefault(variableName, 0) + 1);
                    if (stringAppendsCount.get(variableName) > 1) {
                        addViolation(data, assignment);
                    }
                }
            } else {
                visitChild(child, data);
            }
        }
        return data;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private Map<String, Integer> variableUsageCount = new HashMap<>();

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentOperator node, Object data) {
        if (node.isCompound()) {
            Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();
            if (parent instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                String varName = ((ASTVariableAccess) parent).getVariableName();
                int count = variableUsageCount.getOrDefault(varName, 0);
                variableUsageCount.put(varName, count + 1);
                if (count >= 2) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private Map<String, Integer> stringVariables = new HashMap<>();

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTVariableDeclaratorId.class, ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTVariableDeclaratorId node, Object data) {
        if ("String".equals(node.getNameDeclaration().getTypeImage())) {
            stringVariables.put(node.getImage(), 0);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        String variableName = node.jjtGetChild(0).jjtGetChild(0).getImage();
        if (stringVariables.containsKey(variableName) && node.isCompound()) {
            int count = stringVariables.get(variableName);
            stringVariables.put(variableName, ++count);
            if (count > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.Objects;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.isAdditive()) {
            Node parent = node.getNthParent(2);
            if (parent instanceof ASTBlock) {
                Node sibling = node.getPreviousSibling();
                if (sibling != null && sibling instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression
                        && Objects.equals(((ASTAssignmentExpression) sibling).getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class).getImage(),
                        node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class).getImage())) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    private Map<String, Integer> variableUsageCount = new HashMap<>();

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        Node firstChild = node.jjtGetChild(0);

        if (firstChild instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
            String variableName = ((ASTVariableAccess) firstChild).getFirstDescendantOfType(JavaNode.class).getImage();
            variableUsageCount.put(variableName, variableUsageCount.getOrDefault(variableName, 0) + 1);

            if (variableUsageCount.get(variableName) > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        Node parentNode = node.jjtGetParent();
        if (parentNode instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
            Node leftHandSide = node.jjtGetChild(0);
            Node rightHandSide = node.jjtGetChild(1);
            if (leftHandSide instanceof ASTVariableAccess && rightHandSide instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                String name = ((ASTVariableAccess) leftHandSide).getImage();
                String parentName = ((ASTVariableAccess) parentNode.jjtGetChild(0)).getImage();
                if (parentName.equals(name)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

                addViolation(data, node);

        }

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTInitializer.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTExpressionStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        visitChildren(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        visitChildren(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpressionStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2 &&
                node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess &&
                node.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTStringLiteral &&
                ((ASTVariableAccess) node.jjtGetChild(0)).jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableDeclaratorId &&
                ((ASTVariableAccess) node.jjtGetChild(0)).jjtGetChild(0).jjtGetNumChildren() == 1 &&
                ((ASTVariableAccess) node.jjtGetChild(0)).jjtGetChild(0).jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTAssignmentOperator &&
                "+=".equals(((ASTAssignmentOperator) ((ASTVariableAccess) node.jjtGetChild(0)).jjtGetChild(0).jjtGetChild(0)).getImage())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void visitChildren(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            node.jjtGetChild(i).jjtAccept(this, data);
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private int count = 0;
    private String previousVariableName = "";

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentOperator node, Object data) {
        if (node.getImage().equals("+=")) {
            Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();
            String currentVariableName = parent.jjtGetChild(0).getImage();
            if (currentVariableName.equals(previousVariableName)) {
                count++;
                if (count > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            } else {
                count = 0;
            }
            previousVariableName = currentVariableName;
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTExpressionStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        int appendCount = 0;
        NodeStream nodeStream = node.children();
        while (nodeStream.hasNext()) {
            Node child = nodeStream.next();
            if (child instanceof ASTExpressionStatement) {
                appendCount += countAppends((ASTExpressionStatement) child);
            }
        }
        if (appendCount > 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private int countAppends(ASTExpressionStatement node) {
        int appendCount = 0;
        NodeStream nodeStream = node.children();
        while (nodeStream.hasNext()) {
            Node child = nodeStream.next();
            if (child instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
                ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentNode = (ASTAssignmentExpression) child;
                if (assignmentNode.jjtGetFirstToken().image.equals("+=")) {
                    appendCount++;
                }
            }
        }
        return appendCount;
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpressionStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        int appendCount = node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class).size();

        if (appendCount > 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;

            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentOperator node, Object data) {
        if (node.isCompound()) {
            Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();
            String variableName = parent.jjtGetChild(0).jjtGetChild(0).getImage();
            String variableValue = parent.jjtGetChild(1).jjtGetChild(0).getImage();
            if (variableName.equals(variableValue)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTForStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        int numAppends = node.getNumChildrenOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (numAppends > 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator().equals("+=")) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTBlock && 
            (node.jjtGetParent().jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTForeachStatement || 
             node.jjtGetParent().jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTWhileStatement)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 6
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        Node parentNode = node.jjtGetParent();
        if (parentNode instanceof ASTBlock) {
            parentNode = parentNode.jjtGetParent();
            if (parentNode instanceof ASTWhileStatement || parentNode instanceof ASTForeachStatement) {
                checkForViolation(node, data);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkForViolation(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        Node firstChild = node.jjtGetChild(0);
        Node secondChild = node.jjtGetChild(1);
        if (firstChild instanceof ASTVariableAccess && secondChild instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTBlock.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        checkConcatenation(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        checkConcatenation(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        checkConcatenation(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkConcatenation(Node node, Object data) {
        int numConcatenations = node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class).size();
        if (numConcatenations > 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
    }
}

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if(containsStringConcatenation(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if(containsStringConcatenation(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean containsStringConcatenation(ASTBlock node) {
        return node.findChildrenOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class)
                .stream()
                .anyMatch(op -> "+=".equals(op.getImage()));
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTBlock.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        checkStringAppends(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        checkStringAppends(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        checkStringAppends(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkStringAppends(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        for (ASTAssignmentExpression ae : node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)) {
            if (ae.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) != null) {
                addViolation(data, ae);
            }
        }
    }

    private void checkStringAppends(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        for (ASTAssignmentExpression ae : node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)) {
            if (ae.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) != null) {
                addViolation(data, ae);
            }
        }
    }

    private void checkStringAppends(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        for (ASTAssignmentExpression ae : node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)) {
            if (ae.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) != null) {
                addViolation(data, ae);
            }
        }
    }
}

==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: various concats in loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {
    public String bad() {
        String description = " " + ";";
        List<String> persons = new ArrayList<String>();
        for (final String person : persons) {
            if (person != null) {
                description += "0" + ":"; //bad
            } else {
                description += ":"; //bad
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTMethodDeclaration.class, ASTBlock.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(final ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, final Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(final ASTMethodDeclaration node, final Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(final ASTBlock node, final Object data) {
        int stringAppendsCount = 0;

        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            Node childNode = node.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (childNode instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
                ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = (ASTAssignmentExpression) childNode;
                if (assignmentExpression.getOperator().equals("+=") &&
                        assignmentExpression.jjtGetChild(0).getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) != null) {
                    stringAppendsCount++;
                }
            }
        }

        if (stringAppendsCount > 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
            description += ";"; // bad
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class).forEach(loop -> {
            loop.findDescendantsOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class).forEach(assign -> {
                if(assign.hasImageEqualTo("+=")) {
                    if(assign.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) != null) {
                        addViolation(data, assign);
                    }
                }
            });
        });
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        boolean foundStringAppends = false;

        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            if (node.jjtGetChild(i) instanceof ASTBlock) {
                ASTBlock block = (ASTBlock) node.jjtGetChild(i);

                for (int j = 0; j < block.jjtGetNumChildren(); j++) {
                    if (block.jjtGetChild(j) instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
                        ASTAssignmentExpression assignExpression = (ASTAssignmentExpression) block.jjtGetChild(j);

                        if (assignExpression.jjtGetChild(0).getImage().equals("+=")) {
                            if (!foundStringAppends) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                                foundStringAppends = true;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private static final PropertyDescriptor<Integer> CONSECUTIVE_APPENDS_DESCRIPTOR
            = PropertyFactory.intProperty("consecutiveAppendsThreshold")
            .desc("The number of consecutive appends which trigger a violation")
            .defaultValue(2)
            .build();

    private int consecutiveAppends;

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        definePropertyDescriptor(CONSECUTIVE_APPENDS_DESCRIPTOR);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        consecutiveAppends = 0;
        super.visit(node, data);
        checkViolation(data);
        return data;
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        consecutiveAppends = 0;
        super.visit(node, data);
        checkViolation(data);
        return data;
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        consecutiveAppends = 0;
        super.visit(node, data);
        checkViolation(data);
        return data;
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpressionStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isStringAppend(node)) {
            consecutiveAppends++;
        } else {
            consecutiveAppends = 0;
        }
        super.visit(node, data);
        checkViolation(data);
        return data;
    }

    private void checkViolation(Object data) {
        if (consecutiveAppends >= propertyDescriptor(CONSECUTIVE_APPENDS_DESCRIPTOR)) {
            addViolation(data, (AbstractNode) data);
        }
    }

    private boolean isStringAppend(ASTExpressionStatement node) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 0) {
            return false;
        }

        if (node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTAssignmentOperator) {
            ASTAssignmentOperator operator = (ASTAssignmentOperator) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            return Objects.equals(operator.getImage(), "+=");
        }

        return false;
    }
}

```
public class ConcatInLoop {
    public String bad() {
        String description = " " + ";";
        List<String> persons = new ArrayList<String>();
        for (final String person : persons) {
            if (person != null) {
                description += "0" + ":"; //bad
            } else {
                description += ":"; //bad
            }
            description += person.toString() + ":"; // bad
            description += ";"; // bad
            description += person.toString(); // bad
        }
        return description;
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;
import java.util.Objects;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentOperator node, Object data) {
        if (node.isCompound()) {
            Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();
            if (parent instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
                Node target = parent.jjtGetChild(0);
                if (target instanceof ASTName) {
                    ASTName name = (ASTName) target;
                    if (!Objects.equals(name.getImage(), "StringBuilder.append") && !Objects.equals(name.getImage(), "StringBuffer.append")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTDoStatement.class).stream()
            .filter(doNode -> doNode.findDescendantsOfType(ASTExpressionStatement.class).stream()
                .anyMatch(expNode -> {
                    ASTAssignmentOperator assOp = expNode.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
                    ASTInfixExpression infixExp = expNode.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                    return assOp != null && infixExp != null && assOp.isCompound() && "+".equals(infixExp.getOperator());
                })
            )
            .forEach(badNode -> addViolation(data, badNode));
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        Node block = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class);
        if (block != null) {
            for (ASTDoStatement doStatement : block.findDescendantsOfType(ASTDoStatement.class)) {
                checkStringConcat(doStatement, data);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkStringConcat(ASTDoStatement doStatement, Object data) {
        for (ASTAssignmentOperator assignment : doStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class)) {
            if (assignment.getImage().equals("+=")) {
                for (ASTInfixExpression infix : assignment.findDescendantsOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class)) {
                    if (infix.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
                        addViolation(data, infix);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
        ASTVariableAccess variable = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
        ASTVariableDeclaratorId varDeclaratorId = variable.getFirstParentOfType(ASTVariableDeclaratorId.class);
        return varDeclaratorId != null && "String".equals(varDeclaratorId.getTypeNode().getTypeImage());
    }
    return false;
  }
}

            logStatement = logStatement + values.get(i++) + ", "; // bad
        } while (i < values.length());
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
        if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
    }

    private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        return node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) &&
                node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) &&
                "String".equals(node.getVariableAccess().getTypeImage());
    }
}

===============================新加一个测试用例生成的checker repair_test_error_query_when_testing==========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
  }
}
```

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) && 
           node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) &&
           node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class).getType().equals(String.class);
  }
}

You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
  }
}
```

public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    addRuleChainVisit(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.hasDescendantOfType(JavaParserTreeConstants.JJTSTRINGLITERAL);

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;

public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node) && isStringType(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
  }

  private boolean isStringType(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class).getType() == String.class;
  }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
        if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
    }

    private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        ASTAssignmentOperator operator = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
        if (operator != null && operator.isCompound()) {
            for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
                Node child = node.jjtGetChild(i);
                if (child instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                    return true;
                }
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.Map;
import java.util.HashMap;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private final Map<String, String> lastOperation = new HashMap<>();

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() >= 2 && node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            String varName = varAccess.getName();

            if (node.getOperator().equals("+=")) {
                if (lastOperation.getOrDefault(varName, "").equals("+=")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                } else {
                    lastOperation.put(varName, "+=");
                }
            } else if (node.getOperator().equals("=")) {
                lastOperation.put(varName, "=");
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() >= 2 &&
                node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTName &&
                node.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTAssignmentOperator) {

            ASTAssignmentOperator op = (ASTAssignmentOperator) node.jjtGetChild(1);
            if (op.isCompound()) {
                checkForStringType(node, data);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkForStringType(ASTExpression node, Object data) {
        String varName = ((ASTName) node.jjtGetChild(0)).getImage();
        Node varDeclaration = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTVariableDeclaratorId.class);
        if (varDeclaration != null && varName.equals(((ASTVariableDeclaratorId) varDeclaration).getImage())) {
            String varType = ((ASTVariableDeclaratorId) varDeclaration).getNameDeclaration().getTypeImage();
            if ("String".equals(varType)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
  }
}
```

    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class) && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)
            && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class);
  }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
      ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
      String varType = varAccess.getType().getName();
      return varType.equals("java.lang.String");
    }
    return false;
  }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringType(node.jjtGetChild(0))) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringType(Node node) {
    if (node instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
        ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node;
        return variableAccess.getType().equals(String.class);
    }
    return false;
  }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTAdditiveExpression.class) && 
           node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class);
  }

```
// Test new rule example
public class Foo {

                        result += getStringFromSomeWhere(i);
                    }
                    return result;
```
