package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
        if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
            node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
            node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
            node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
    }

    private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        return (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) || 
            (node.jjtGetChild(0).jjtGetChild(0).jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTInfixExpression);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    if(node.getOperator() == ASTAssignmentExpression.Operator.ADDITION_ASSIGN) {
      if(node.getType() == String.class) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
        if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
    }

    private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        if (node.isCompound()) {
            ASTPrimaryExpression primaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTPrimaryExpression.class);
            if (primaryExpression != null) {
                ASTName name = primaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTName.class);
                if (name != null) {
                    NameOccurrence no = name.getNameDeclaration().getUsages().iterator().next();
                    if (no.getLocation().getType().equals(String.class)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isMultipleStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isMultipleStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    int count = node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class).size();
    return count > 1;
  }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
        if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
    }

    private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class)) {
            ASTAssignmentOperator operator = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
            return operator.isCompound() && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
        }
        return false;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
        if (isInLoop(node) && isRepeatedStringConcatenation(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
    }

    private boolean isRepeatedStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
            ASTName left = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTName.class);
            ASTName right = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class).getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTName.class);
            return left != null && right != null && left.hasImageEqualTo(right.getImage());
        }
        return false;
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;

      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {

           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentOperator node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isCompound()) {
            return super.visit(node, data);
        }

        ASTName name = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTName.class);
        if (name == null || name.getType() != String.class) {
            return super.visit(node, data);
        }

        for (NameOccurrence no : name.getUsages()) {
            if (isInLoop(no.getLocation())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
                return super.visit(node, data);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isInLoop(Node node) {
        return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;



import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    if (node.getOperator().equals("+=")) {
      ASTName astName = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTName.class);
      if (astName != null) {
        for (NameOccurrence occurrence : astName.getUsages()) {
          VariableNameDeclaration declaration = (VariableNameDeclaration) occurrence.getLocation();
          if (declaration.getTypeImage().equals("String")) {
            return true;
          }
        }
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) &&
           node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) &&
           !(node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTLiteral.class) != null && node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2) &&
           !(node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null && node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2);
  }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
      ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class).get(0);
      if (ASTStringLiteral.class.isAssignableFrom(variableAccess.getType())) {
        return node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return "+=".equals(node.getOperator()) 
            && (node.isLeftHandSideType(ASTVariableAccess.class) 
            && (node.isRightHandSideType(ASTStringLiteral.class) 
            || node.isRightHandSideType(ASTVariableAccess.class)));
  }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentOperator node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentOperator node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentOperator node) {
    return node.hasImage("+=") && node.jjtGetParent().hasDescendantOfType(ASTAdditiveExpression.class);
  }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    if(node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class)) {
      final ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
      return "+".equals(infixExpression.getOperator()) && infixExpression.jjtGetNumChildren() > 1;
    }
    return false;
  }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
  }

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    private Map<String, Integer> varCounter = new HashMap<>();

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        varCounter.clear();
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
        if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
    }

    private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class)) {
            ASTVariableAccess var = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (var != null) {
                String varName = var.getVariableName();
                varCounter.put(varName, varCounter.getOrDefault(varName, 0) + 1);
                return varCounter.get(varName) > 1;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class)) {
      ASTInfixExpression infix = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
      return "+".equals(infix.getOperator()) && infix.getFirstChildOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class) != null;
    }
    return false;
  }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.HashSet;
import java.util.Set;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
        if (isInLoop(node) && isRepeatedStringConcatenation(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
    }

    private boolean isRepeatedStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        if(node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
            Set<String> variableNames = new HashSet<>();
            for(ASTVariableAccess variableAccess : node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
                if(!variableNames.add(variableAccess.getVariableName())) {
                    return true;
                }
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
        if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node) && isStringType(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
                node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
    }

    private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        ASTInfixExpression infix = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        return infix != null && infix.getOperator() == JavaParserConstants.ADD;
    }

    private boolean isStringType(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        return TypeHelper.isA(node, String.class);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
  }
}
```

public class UseStringBuffer {
    public void foo() {
        String value = "";
        value = (value != null) ? "1" : "0";
    }
}
This checker has passed this negative testcase:
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        int i = 0;
        do {
            logStatement = logStatement + values.get(i++) + ", "; // bad
        } while (i < values.length());
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;



import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

  public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
    super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
  }

  @Override
  public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
    if (isInLoop(node) && isStringConcatenation(node)) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }

  private boolean isInLoop(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null ||
           node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null;
  }

  private boolean isStringConcatenation(final ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
    ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    return infixExpression != null && "+".equals(infixExpression.getOperator()) && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
  }
}
